-- 11001 //유방암 환자수
INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT HCODE AS HOSP_CD, PTNO AS PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(FDX,1,4) AS CRIT_YR,  
CASE WHEN AGE<'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN AGE<'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN AGE<'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN AGE<'50' THEN 40  --40대 
     WHEN AGE<'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN AGE<'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN AGE<'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN AGE>='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상 
   END AS PT_AGE,
SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, POPCODE AS STATS_TRGT_VL
FROM (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, MIN(AGE) AS AGE, SEX, MIN(FDX) AS FDX, POPCODE FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE POPCODE = '05' GROUP BY HCODE, PTNO,SEX, POPCODE) A -- '05' 유방암
WHERE FDX BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)
SELECT 11001 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 환자수' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 99010 AS TBL_ID, 9901002 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A 
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT 
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B 
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD;


-- 11002 //유방암 음주여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.CUR_DRNK_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.CUR_DRNK_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11002 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 음주여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101006 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11003 //유방암 음주력여부별

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대

   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DHIS_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DHIS_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체

cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM

-- 11007 //유방암 음주횟수별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRNK_NT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRNK_NT,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11007 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 음주횟수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11013 //유방암 흡연량별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.SMOK_QTY as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.SMOK_QTY,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11013 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 흡연량별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101022 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MHIS_DBT_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MHIS_DBT_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11018 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 병력당뇨여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101029 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11024 //유방암 병력우울증여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.ADM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.MHIS_DEPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.MHIS_DEPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11024 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 병력우울증여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101041 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ADM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OHAD_HSTR_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.OHAD_HSTR_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_HLINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ADM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11031 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 타병원진단후전원여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11010 AS TBL_ID, 1101053 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11038 //유방암 가족력결핵여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.FMHT_RCRD_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.FMHT_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.FMHT_TB_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.FMHT_TB_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_FMHT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.FMHT_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11038 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 가족력결핵여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11020 AS TBL_ID, 1102014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.HRPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.HRPR_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_OBINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OBTR_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11046 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 HRT경험여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11030 AS TBL_ID, 1103009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

-- 11052 //유방암 모유수유월수별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OBTR_RCRD_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.BRFD_MCNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.BRFD_MCNT),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM BRCN_PT_OBINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OBTR_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OBTR_RCRD_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OBTR_RCRD_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.UTEC_YN_NOANS_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.UTEC_YN_NOANS_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_PT_OBINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OBTR_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11057 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 자궁적출술여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11030 AS TBL_ID, 1103024 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ifnull(A.CTRT_BLPR_VL,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_DIAG_ANINF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ANTH_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11062 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 수축혈압별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11040 AS TBL_ID, 1104009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11068 //유방암 진단SNOMEDCT명별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DIAG_RGST_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DIAG_RGST_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DIAG_SMCT_NM as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DIAG_SMCT_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_DIAG_INF A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DIAG_RGST_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11068 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 진단SNOMEDCT명별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11050 AS TBL_ID, 1105012 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ifnull(A.AJCC_YR,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_DIAG_STAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DIAG_STAG_RCRD_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11079 //유방암 진단검사EDI코드별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.CEXM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.CEXM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.CEXM_EDI_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.CEXM_EDI_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_DIAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.CEXM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11079 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 진단검사EDI코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11080 AS TBL_ID, 1108009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C

ifnull(A.CEXM_LOINC_NM,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_DIAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.CEXM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11084 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 진단검사LOINC명별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11080 AS TBL_ID, 1108014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.IMEX_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEX_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.BRST_DENS_CLCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.BRST_DENS_CLCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_IMAG A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.IMEX_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11090 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 유방밀도분류별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11090 AS TBL_ID, 1109014 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BPSY_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO

CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.IMEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.IMEM_OPN_CLCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.IMEM_OPN_CLCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_IMPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.IMEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11101 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 면역병리검사소견분류별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11110 AS TBL_ID, 1111010 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.GMVX_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DNA_VAINF_C_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DNA_VAINF_C_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_GMVX A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.GMVX_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11112 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 DNA변이정보C별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11130 AS TBL_ID, 1113019 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11118 //유방암 수술종류별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.OPRT_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OPRT_KNCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.OPRT_KNCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.OPRT_ICD9CM_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.OPRT_ICD9CM_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11123 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 수술ICD9CM코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11150 AS TBL_ID, 1115013 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.OPRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상

ifnull(A.BRCN_OPRT_MTCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO

)

FROM BRCN_TRTM_OPRT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.OPRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.BLTR_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.BLTR_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.BLTR_PACK_CNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.BLTR_PACK_CNT),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM BRCN_TRTM_BLTR A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.BLTR_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11140 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 수혈팩수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11160 AS TBL_ID, 1116010 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상

B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.TUMR_WDTH_LNTH_VL as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.TUMR_WDTH_LNTH_VL),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM BRCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11145 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 종양가로길이별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117011 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11151 //유방암 림프혈관침윤존재여부별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.LVIN_EX_YN_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.LVIN_EX_YN_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11151 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 림프혈관침윤존재여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117019 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.INCN_ASSO_EX_YN_SPCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.INCN_ASSO_EX_YN_SPCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11156 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 상피내암동반존재여부별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117029 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11162 //유방암 잔여종양별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RESI_TUMR_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RESI_TUMR_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11162 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 잔여종양별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117040 AS COL_ID,

TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

-- 11167 //유방암 비감시림프절총수별

(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.SRGC_PTEM_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.NSND_TOTL_CNT as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(TO_CHAR(A.NSND_TOTL_CNT),'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NUMERIC 컬럼 변환(NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체)
FROM BRCN_EXAM_SGPT A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11167 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 비감시림프절총수별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117046 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.SRGC_PTEM_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11172 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 수술후병리N병기별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11170 AS TBL_ID, 1117051 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11178 //유방암 약제성분종류별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRIN_KNCD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRIN_KNCD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_DRIN A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11178 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 약제성분종류별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11190 AS TBL_ID, 1119009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRUG_EDI_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.DRUG_EDI_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_DRIN A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11183 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 약제EDI코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11190 AS TBL_ID, 1119017 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11189 //유방암 약제처방용량단위별

WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.DRUG_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.DRUG_PRSC_CAPA_UNIT_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL,

ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.DRUG_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
)

INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.ANTP_STRT_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.ANTP_END_RESN_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.ANTP_END_RESN_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_ANTP A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.ANTP_STRT_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11194 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 항암요법종료이유별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11200 AS TBL_ID, 1120011 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11200 //유방암 방사선치료EDI코드별

INSERT INTO CNCR_TBL_SMRY_STATS
(SMRY_STATS_NO, HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, SMRY_STATS_NM, TBL_ID, COL_ID, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, NCS, WHOL_NCS, PT_CNT, WHOL_PT_CNT, STATS_WORK_YMD, COLL_STRT_YMD, COLL_END_YMD, CRTN_DT) 
WITH W1 AS (
SELECT A.HOSP_CD, A.PT_SBST_NO, SUBSTRING(A.RDT_PRSC_YMD,1,4) AS CRIT_YR, 
CASE WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'20' THEN 10 --20세 미만
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RDT_EDI_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RDT_EDI_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_RD A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RDT_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11200 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 방사선치료EDI코드별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11210 AS TBL_ID, 1121009 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;

     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'30' THEN 20  --20대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'40' THEN 30  --30대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'50' THEN 40  --40대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'60' THEN 50  --50대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'70' THEN 60  --60대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25) <'80' THEN 70  --70대
     WHEN FLOOR(DAYS_BETWEEN(b.BRTH, a.RDT_PRSC_YMD)/365.25)  >='80' THEN 80  --80대 이상
   END AS PT_AGE,
B.SEX AS PT_SEX_CD, A.RDT_SITE_CD as STATS_TRGT_COL, 
ifnull(A.RDT_SITE_CD,'#N/A' ) AS STATS_TRGT_VL -- NULL은 '#N/A'로 대체
FROM BRCN_TRTM_RD A
INNER JOIN (SELECT DISTINCT HCODE, PTNO, ADD_DAYS(BRTH, 14) AS BRTH, SEX FROM CNCR_RGST WHERE BRTH IS NOT NULL AND POPCODE = '05' ) B -- '05' 유방암
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HCODE
AND A.PT_SBST_NO = B.PTNO
AND A.RDT_PRSC_YMD BETWEEN '20100101' AND '20211231'
) 
SELECT 11205 AS SMRY_STATS_NO, A.HOSP_CD, A.CRIT_YR, '유방암 방사선치료부위별' AS SMRY_STATS_NM, 11210 AS TBL_ID, 1121015 AS COL_ID,
cast(A.PT_AGE as INTEGER) as PT_AGE, A.PT_SEX_CD, A.STATS_TRGT_VL, A.NCS,  B.WHOL_NCS, A.PT_CNT, B.WHOL_PT_CNT, 
TO_CHAR(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,'YYYYMMDD') AS STATS_WORK_YMD, '20100101' AS COLL_STRT_YMD, '20211231' AS COLL_END_YMD, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS CRTN_DT FROM 
(SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, STATS_TRGT_VL) AS A  
INNER JOIN (SELECT HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, COUNT(STATS_TRGT_VL) AS WHOL_NCS, COUNT(DISTINCT PT_SBST_NO) AS  WHOL_PT_CNT
FROM W1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) AS B  
ON A.HOSP_CD = B.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=B.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = B.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = B.PT_SEX_CD  
INNER JOIN (select HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD, count(STATS_TRGT_COL) as STATS_TRGT_CNT from w1 GROUP BY HOSP_CD, CRIT_YR, PT_AGE, PT_SEX_CD) C  
ON A.HOSP_CD = C.HOSP_CD AND A.CRIT_YR=C.CRIT_YR AND A.PT_AGE = C.PT_AGE AND A.PT_SEX_CD = C.PT_SEX_CD where C.STATS_TRGT_CNT <> 0;


-- 11206 //유방암 방사선선량별
